wikipedia wikidata mismatch - follow wikipedia redirect - for parish prefixed tags
parish:wikidata and parish:wikipedia tags link to a different objects, because parish:wikipedia tag points to a redirect that should be followed
Q22443353 vs (missing) article redirects from pl:Parafia św. Jana XXIII w Wirach to pl:Parafia św. Jana XXIII w Komornikach
Kościół pw. Świętego Jana XXIII - an affected OSM element that may be improved

overpass query usable in JOSM that will load all objects where this specific error is present:
[out:xml][timeout:3600]; ( way(693895082)['parish:wikidata'='Q22443353']['parish:wikipedia'='pl:Parafia św. Jana XXIII w Wirach']; ); (._;>;); out meta qt;//['wikipedia wikidata mismatch - follow wikipedia redirect - for parish prefixed tags']
